<details>
<summary>Rating scale (6/6 best → 1/6 worst)</summary>

- **6/6 Confirmed** — Reproduced against current main — the failing behavior was observed directly, or a commenter supplied a confirmed reproduction.
- **5/6 Source-confirmed** — Traced conclusively in the current source via a checkout — the buggy code path is identified, though not executed.
- **4/6 Traced** — A likely defect path was found in the source, but with some uncertainty that it's the true cause.
- **3/6 Plausible** — The report reads as coherent and credible, but it wasn't reproduced or traced in the code — not yet verified.
- **2/6 Unverified** — A genuine reproduction attempt failed, or the report is too thin to verify.
- **1/6 Inconclusive** — Signals conflict — a reproduction was claimed but confidence is low; treat the rating with caution.
- **—** — not a bug (nothing to rate).

</details>
